 *** Dussehra i
e
 Vijayadashami is a major festival of Hindus
 aswin maas ke shukla paksh kii dashami tithi ko iskaa aayojan hota he
 Lord Rama killed Ravana on this day
 ise asaty par satya kii vijay ke rup main manaaya jaataa he
 That is why this Dashami is known as Vijayadashami
 isi din log nayaa kaary prarambh karte hai, shastr-puja kii jaati he
 In ancient times, kings used to go on a battle march on this day praying for victory
 is din jagah-jagah meley lagate hai
 Ramlila is organized
 ravan kaa vishaal putala banaakar use jalaayaa jaataa he
 Dussehra or Vijayadashami is celebrated as the victory of Lord Rama
 yah shastr pujan kii tithi bhi he
 It is a festival of joy and joy and victory
 dashahra par deshbhar main yojit hoti hai ramlilaenbhagwan ram kii ravan par vijay ke uplakshya main manaaya jane vaala dashahra buraai par achchhai kii vijay kaa pratik he
 Earlier Ramlila is organized at many places during Navratri
 dilli main aitihaasik laal kile ke sameep ramlila maidan ke alaava anek anya sthanon par ravan, uske bhai kumbhakarna or bete meghnad ke vishalkay putale kaa dahan hota he
 The belief behind doing this is that religion has won over unrighteousness and truth has won over untruth
 is din hajaaron log yahaan upasthit hote hai
 On this day, enthusiasm is seen in people all over the country
 samay ke saath-saath ramlilaon ko pesh karne ke tareeke, unke str or quality main bhi lagaataar badlaav aata rahaa he
 Modern techniques are being used in staging Ramlila today
 ramlilaon ke kai seen tamaam modern takneekon or computer ke jariye kuch is tarah pesh kiye ja rahe hai ki ve hakeekat ko chhu leti hai
 While the effigies are burnt electronically in Lila of Lal Qila, computerized buildings are also seen in Ramlila in other parts of the country
 jahaan ek taraf ramlilaon ke yuddh drishyon main talavaaron se chingaariyaan nikalati hai or agni tir chalaae jate hai vahiin milaap ke drishyon ko bahut maarmik tareeke se pesh kiya jaataa he
 Viewers are also taken care of not boredom
 kumbhakarna ko gahari nidra se jagaane kaa seen kuch isi tarah kaa hota he
 Kumbhakarna is awakened by a crane sleeping in a deep sleep during the war of Lanka
 jis tarah se ramlila dekhne waalon kii bheed jutati he ham kah sakate hai ki desh main aaj bhi ramlila kaa anand apane charam par virajman he
 Over time, some techniques are used to try to add more viewers
 kya he dashahra kaa saamaajik mahatva?dashahara kaa saanskrithik pahalu bhi he
 India is an agricultural country
 jab kisaan apane khet main sunahari fasal ugaakar anaaj rupi sampatti ghar laata he to uske ullas or umang kii koi seemaa nahin rahati

 puure bharatvarsh main yah parv vibhinn pradeshon main vibhinn prakaar se manaaya jaataa he

 kaise manaate hai bharat ke vibhinn pradeshon main dashahra?dashahra athwa vijaydashami ram kii vijay ke rup main manaaya jaae athwa durga puja ke rup main, donon hi roopon main yah shakti puja kaa parv he
 Arms are also worshiped on this day
 yah harsh or ullas tathaa vijay kaa parv he
 It is celebrated in different ways in every corner of the country
 :-1
 Dussehra of Kullu is very famous in Himachal Pradesh
 anya sthanon kii hi bhaanti yahaan bhi das din athwa ek saptaah pehle se hi is parv kii taiyaari aarambh ho jaati he

 saath hi ve apane mukhya devtaa raghunatha ji kii bhi puja karte hai
 The dancers trained in this procession perform the dance
 is prakaar juluus banaakar nagar ke mukhya bhaagon se hote hue nagar parikrama karte hai or kullu nagar main devtaa raghunathji kii vandana se dashahara ke utsav kaa aarambh karte hai
 The beauty of this festival is unique on Dashami
 2
 In Punjab, Dussehra is celebrated by fasting for nine days of Navratri
 is dauraan yahaan aagantukon kaa swaagat paaramparik mithai or uphaaron se kiya jaataa he

 3
 Not considering the main cause of Dussehra in Bastar as 'rama's victory over Ravana', people consider it a festival dedicated to the worship of Mother Danteshwari
 danteshwari mata bastar anchal ke nivaasiyon kii aradhy devi hai, jo durga kaa hi rup hai
 The Dussehra here runs from Amavas of Shravan month to Shukla Trayodashi of Ashwin month
 pratham din devi se samaaroh aarambh karne kii anumati lee jaati he
 The goddess sits on a bed of thorns
 yah kanya ek anusuchit jati kii he, jisase bastar ke rajpariwaar ke vyakti anumati lete hai
 The ceremony began around the fifteenth century
 4
 In Bengal, Orissa and Assam, this festival is celebrated as Durga Puja
 yah bengaaliyon, urisa or assam ke logon kaa sabase mahatvapurn tyohaar he
 This festival is celebrated for five days all over Bengal
 urisa or assam main chaar din tak tyohaar chalata he
 Here Goddess Durga is ensconced in grandly decorated pandals
 desh ke nami kalakaaron ko bulawaakar durga kii murti taiyaar karwaai jaati hai
 Along with this, many idols of other deities are also made
 tyohaar ke dauraan shahar main chote mote stall bhi mithaiyon se bhare rahete hai

 are organized
 uske uparaant saptami, ashtami evam navami ke din praatah or siankal durga kii puja main vyateet hote hai

 dashami ke din vishesh puja kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 Men embrace each other
 striyaan devi ke maathe par sindur chadhaati hai or saath hi aapas main sindur bhi lagaati hai
 It is considered very auspicious to see Neelkanth bird here on this day
 iske baad devi kii pratimaaon ko visarjeet kiya jaataa he
 5
 tamilnadu, andhra pradesh evam karnataka main dashahra nau dinon tak chalata he jisamen teen deviyaan lakshmi, saraswati or durga kii puja karte hai
 The first three days are worshiped by Lakshmi, the goddess of wealth and prosperity
 agle teen din saraswati, kala or vidya kii devi, kii archana kii jaati he or antim din devi durga, shakti kii devi, kii stuti kii jaati he
 The place of worship is well decorated with flowers and lamps
 log ek duusare ko mithaiyaan or kapade dete hai
 Mysore's Dussehra in Karnataka is particularly notable
 mysore main dashahara ke samay puure shahar kii galiyon ko roshni se sajjit kiya jaataa he or haathiyon kaa shringaar kar puure shahar main ek bhavy juluus nikaala jaataa he
 At this time the famous Mysore palace is decorated like a bride from Deepmalika
 iske saath shahar main log tarch lite ke sang nrity or sangeet kii shobhaa yatra kaa anand lete hai
 Let us tell you one thing here that ravana-dahan is not organized in these Dravidian regions
 6
 In Gujarat, the clay is considered a symbol of the graceful colorful pitcher goddess and it is a popular dance called garba, with virgin girls holding it over their heads
 garba nrity is parv kii shaan he
 Men and women dance in a circle, playing two small colored poles to the rhythm of music
 is avasar par bhakthi, film tathaa paaramparik lok-sangeet sabhi kaa samaayojan hota he
 After Pooja and Aarti, Dandiya Raas is held all night
 navaratri main sone or gahanon kii kharid ko shubh mana jaataa he
 7
 maharashtra main navaratri ke nau din maa durga ko samarpit rahete hai, jabaki dasven din gyaan kii devi saraswati kii vandana kii jaati he
 On this day, school going children worship the tantric symbols of Maa Saraswati to get blessings in their studies
 kisi bhi cheez ko prarambh karne ke liye khaskar vidya aarambh karne ke liye yah din kaaphi shubh mana jaataa he
 People of Maharashtra consider this day to be an auspicious time to marry, enter home and buy new homes

 soochna ayukta yashovardhan aaazaad ne yah aadesh artiai kaaryakarta nutan thakur ke aavedan par diya
 He had sought details of criminal cases filed against various IPS officers across the country from the ministry
 apane jawaab main grih mantralay kii police shakha ne kaha he ki ipies adhikariyon ke khilaaf darj aapraadhik maamalon ke bare main mantralay kaa police- 1 divijan file nahin rakhata he
 Azad said, "the PIO said that since the police division of the Ministry of Home Affairs does not maintain such details of criminal cases registered against IPS officers, the question was transferred to the National Crime Records Bureau
 ayog ne jab artiai aavedan ke antaran kii vajah poochi to piaio ne anbhigyata jataai
 '' aaazaad ne gaur kiya ki artiai aavedan ko vivek kaa istemaal kiye bina antarit kiya gaya
 He said, "the NCRB keeps crime figures on a large scale and does not separate the data according to the needs of the appellant
" ‚Äô‚Äô aaazaad ne kaha ki grih mantralay ipies cader kaa mul mantralay hone ke naate kisi adhikari ke khilaaf aarope patr daayar hone par hameshaa soochna praapt karata he
 There are about 9000 officers under the Ministry of Home Affairs across the country
 aaazaad ek purv ipies adhikari hai jo siaisi main shaamil hone se pehle khufia tantra main varisht adhikari ke pad par kaam kar chuke hai
 "despite being allotted the state cadre of the officer, the Ministry of Home Affairs, being the nodal agency, must have the details of the cases registered against the serving IPS officers," he said
 haalanki, piaio ke anusaar vaise ipies adhikariyon ke naamon vaali suchi nahin he, jinke khilaaf aapraadhik maamle darj kiye gaye hai
 '' aaazaad ne mantralay ke adhikari se aapraadhik maamalon kaa saamana kar rahe ipies adhikariyon kii suchi nahin hone ke bayaan ke bare main ek halafanama dene ko kaha
 He said, "as the cadre controlling authority, the role of the Ministry of Home Affairs is to look after the conditions of service of IPS officers

 '' Comments soochna ayukta ne kaha ki mantralay kaa kaam anushaasanamak kaarywahi kii nigaraanee or adhikariyon ke khilaaf jaanch karnaa bhi he
